<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:атакованный.html>атако́ванный</a> (7925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атака.html>ата́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">atáka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атаковать.html>атакова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">atakovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

***атеросклероз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:атеросклероз.html>атеросклероз</a> (18574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">athérosclérose</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атеросклероз.html>атеросклеро́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">atɛroskleróz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атеросклероз.html>атеросклеро́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атеросклероз.html>атеросклеро́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атеросклероз.html>атеросклеро́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> atherosclerosis</li></ol>

***атлетика.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:атлетика.html>атле́тика</a> (22608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атлетика.html>атле́тика</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">atlétika</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атлетика.html>атле́тики</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>athletics
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">лёгкая <a href = vnd.unilang:атлетика.html>атле́тика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ljóxkaja atlétika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">track and field athletics</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:атом.html>а́том</a> (12876)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атом.html>а́том</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">átom</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атом.html>а́тома</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атом.html>а́томы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:атом.html>а́томов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аура.html>а́ура</a> (24521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">aura</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a breeze, a breath of air, the air</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:афганец.html>афга́нец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">afgánec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:афганец.html>афга́нца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:афганец.html>афга́нцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:афганец.html>афга́нцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Afghan (person from Afghanistan)</li>
<li>Afghan (breed of dog)</li>
<li>(in the former Soviet Union) A veteran of the 1979-89 <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Soviet%E2%80%93Afghan_War">Soviet-Afghan War</a></li></ol>
